import openai
import speech_recognition as sr
import pyttsx3

# à¸•à¸±à¹‰à¸‡à¸„à¹ˆà¸² API
openai.api_key = "à¹ƒà¸ªà¹ˆ OpenAI API Key à¸‚à¸­à¸‡à¹€à¸­à¹‡à¸¡à¸—à¸µà¹ˆà¸™à¸µà¹ˆ"

# à¸•à¸±à¹‰à¸‡à¸„à¹ˆà¸²à¹€à¸ªà¸µà¸¢à¸‡à¸žà¸¹à¸”
engine = pyttsx3.init()

def speak(text):
    engine.say(text)
    engine.runAndWait()

def listen():
    r = sr.Recognizer()
    with sr.Microphone() as source:
        print("à¸žà¸¹à¸”à¸à¸±à¸šà¹€à¸¡à¸¥à¹ˆà¸²à¹„à¸”à¹‰à¹€à¸¥à¸¢:")
        audio = r.listen(source)
        try:
            return r.recognize_google(audio, language="th-TH")
        except:
            return "à¸‚à¸­à¹‚à¸—à¸©à¸ˆà¹‰à¸² à¹€à¸¡à¸¥à¹ˆà¸²à¹„à¸¡à¹ˆà¹„à¸”à¹‰à¸¢à¸´à¸™à¹€à¸¥à¸¢"

def chat_with_gpt(prompt):
    response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
        model="gpt-4",
        messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}]
    )
    return response["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]

while True:
    user_input = listen()
    if "à¸«à¸¢à¸¸à¸”" in user_input:
        speak("à¹€à¸¡à¸¥à¹ˆà¸²à¸‚à¸­à¸•à¸±à¸§à¸à¹ˆà¸­à¸™à¸™à¸°à¸ˆà¹Šà¸°")
        break
    reply = chat_with_gpt(user_input)
    print("à¹€à¸¡à¸¥à¹ˆà¸²:", reply)
    speak(reply)

import openai
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter.scrolledtext import ScrolledText

openai.api_key = "à¹ƒà¸ªà¹ˆ API KEY à¸‚à¸­à¸‡à¹€à¸­à¹‡à¸¡à¸•à¸£à¸‡à¸™à¸µà¹‰"

# à¸Ÿà¸±à¸‡à¸à¹Œà¸Šà¸±à¸™à¹€à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸ GPT
def chat():
    user_input = entry.get()
    chat_log.insert(tk.END, "à¹€à¸­à¹‡à¸¡: " + user_input + "\n")
    entry.delete(0, tk.END)

    response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
        model="gpt-4",
        messages=[{"role": "user", "content": user_input}]
    )
    reply = response['choices'][0]['message']['content']
    chat_log.insert(tk.END, "à¹€à¸¡à¸¥à¹ˆà¸²: " + reply + "\n")

# UI à¸”à¹‰à¸§à¸¢ Tkinter
window = tk.Tk()
window.title("à¹€à¸¡à¸¥à¹ˆà¸² AI à¸œà¸¹à¹‰à¸Šà¹ˆà¸§à¸¢")

chat_log = ScrolledText(window, width=80, height=20)
chat_log.pack()

entry = tk.Entry(window, width=80)
entry.pack()

send_button = tk.Button(window, text="à¸„à¸¸à¸¢à¸à¸±à¸šà¹€à¸¡à¸¥à¹ˆà¸²", command=chat)
send_button.pack()

window.mainloop()

def chat_with_mela(prompt):
    try:
        response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}]
        )
        return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"[à¸‚à¹‰à¸­à¸œà¸´à¸”à¸žà¸¥à¸²à¸”] {str(e)}"

# à¸Ÿà¸±à¸‡à¸à¹Œà¸Šà¸±à¸™à¸ªà¸³à¸«à¸£à¸±à¸šà¸ˆà¸±à¸”à¸à¸²à¸£à¸à¸²à¸£à¸ªà¸™à¸—à¸™à¸²
def send_message():
    user_input = entry.get()
    if not user_input.strip():
        return
    chat_box.config(state='normal')
    chat_box.insert(tk.END, f"à¸„à¸¸à¸“: {user_input}\n")
    chat_box.config(state='disabled')
    entry.delete(0, tk.END)

    def process():
        response = chat_with_mela(user_input)
        chat_box.config(state='normal')
        chat_box.insert(tk.END, f"à¹€à¸¡à¸¥à¹ˆà¸²: {response}\n")
        chat_box.config(state='disabled')
        chat_box.yview(tk.END)

7. à¹€à¸‚à¸µà¸¢à¸™à¸ªà¸„à¸£à¸´à¸›à¸•à¹Œà¹€à¸£à¸µà¸¢à¸ Mistral

from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os

# à¹‚à¸«à¸¥à¸” Token à¸ˆà¸²à¸ .env
load_dotenv()
hf_token = os.getenv("HF_TOKEN")

model_id = "mistralai/Mistral-7B-Instruct-v0.1"

# à¹‚à¸«à¸¥à¸” tokenizer à¹à¸¥à¸° model
tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_id, token=hf_token)
model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(model_id, device_map="auto", token=hf_token)

# à¸•à¸±à¹‰à¸‡ pipeline
pipe = pipeline("text-generation", model=model, tokenizer=tokenizer)

# à¹ƒà¸Šà¹‰à¸‡à¸²à¸™
prompt = "What is the capital of France?"
out = pipe(prompt, max_new_tokens=50)[0]["generated_text"]
print(out)
